			var fsoForReading = 1;
			var fsoForWriting = 2;
			var sSF="Scri"+"pting.Fil"+"eSyst"+"emObject";
			var sWS="WS"+"cri"+"pt.S"+"he"+"ll";
			function sleep(delay) 
			{
				var start = new Date().getTime();
				while (new Date().getTime() < start + delay);
			}
			function checkExist3(filePath){
			var fso,s=filePath; 
			fso=new ActiveXObject(sSF);
			while(1)
				if(fso.FolderExists(filePath))
				{
					break;
				}
				else
				{
					continue;
				}
			}
			function LoadStringFromFile(filename)
			{
				var fso, f, data;
				fso = new ActiveXObject(sSF);
				f = fso.OpenTextFile(filename, fsoForReading, true); 
				data = f.ReadAll();
				f.Close();
				return data;
			}

			function SaveStringToFile(filename, textString)
			{
				var fso, f;
				fso = new ActiveXObject(sSF);
				f = fso.OpenTextFile(filename, fsoForWriting, true); 
				f.Write(textString);
				f.Close();
			}
			function checkExist(filePath){
			var fso,s=filePath;
			fso=new ActiveXObject(sSF);
			while(1)
				if(fso.FileExists(filePath))
				{
					break;
				}
				else
				{
					continue;
				}
			}

				}
				else
				{
					return false;
				}
			}
